SELECT TOP(@__p_0) [s].[SessionId], [s].[GroupId], CASE
    WHEN [s].[StartedAt] IS NULL THEN N'Created'
    WHEN [s].[EndedAt] IS NULL THEN N'Active'
    ELSE N'Completed'
END AS [Status], [s].[CreatedAt], (
    SELECT COUNT(*)
    FROM [canvas].[Registrations] AS [r]
    WHERE [s].[SessionId] = [r].[SessionId]) AS [ParticipantCount], CASE
    WHEN EXISTS (
        SELECT 1
        FROM [canvas].[SessionLinks] AS [s0]
        WHERE [s].[SessionId] = [s0].[SessionId]) THEN CONVERT(varchar(36), (
        SELECT TOP(1) [s1].[Guid]
        FROM [canvas].[SessionLinks] AS [s1]
        WHERE [s].[SessionId] = [s1].[SessionId]))
    ELSE N''
